Vertex shader: ../p9/p9.vert
----------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |
 26 |// Atributos del v本tice (sistema de coordenadas del modelo)
 27 |in vec4 position;
 28 |in vec2 texCoord;
 29 |in vec3 normal;
 30 |in vec3 tangent;
 31 |
 32 |// A人de las variables out que necesites
 33 |out vec2 TexCoord;
 34 |out vec3 Lvert;
 35 |out vec3 Vvert;
 36 |
 37 |void main()
 38 |{
 39 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 40 |	vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
 41 |	vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
 42 |	vec3 L;
 43 |	if(lights[0].directional == 0) {
 44 |		L = normalize(vec3(lights[0].positionEye) - eposition);
 45 |	} else {
 46 |		L = normalize(vec3(lights[0].positionEye));
 47 |	}
 48 |	vec3 T = mat3(modelviewMatrix) * tangent;
 49 |	vec3 B = cross(eN, T);
 50 |	vec3 R = mat3(T, B, eN);
 51 |
 52 |	// Propagamos variables
 53 |	Lvert = R * L;
 54 |	Vvert = R * V;
 55 |	TexCoord = vec2(texCoord);
 56 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
 57 |}
 58 |

Vertex shader: ../p9/p9.vert
----------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |
 26 |// Atributos del v本tice (sistema de coordenadas del modelo)
 27 |in vec4 position;
 28 |in vec2 texCoord;
 29 |in vec3 normal;
 30 |in vec3 tangent;
 31 |
 32 |// A人de las variables out que necesites
 33 |out vec2 TexCoord;
 34 |out vec3 Lvert;
 35 |out vec3 Vvert;
 36 |
 37 |void main()
 38 |{
 39 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 40 |	vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
 41 |	vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
 42 |	vec3 L;
 43 |	if(lights[0].directional == 0) {
 44 |		L = normalize(vec3(lights[0].positionEye) - eposition);
 45 |	} else {
 46 |		L = normalize(vec3(lights[0].positionEye));
 47 |	}
 48 |	vec3 T = mat3(modelviewMatrix) * tangent;
 49 |	vec3 B = cross(eN, T);
 50 |	vec3 R = mat3(T, B, eN);
 51 |
 52 |	// Propagamos variables
 53 |	Lvert = R * L;
 54 |	Vvert = R * V;
 55 |	TexCoord = vec2(texCoord);
 56 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
 57 |}
 58 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |uniform float scaleFactor;
 26 |uniform float biasValue;
 27 |
 28 |in vec2 TexCoord;
 29 |in vec3 Lvert;
 30 |in vec3 Vvert;
 31 |out vec4 fragColor;
 32 |
 33 |vec4 iluminacion(vec4 color, vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V, vec3 L) {
 34 |
 35 |    // color = Componente emisiva del material
 36 |
 37 |    // L = Vector iluminaci칩n (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 38 |
 39 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 40 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 41 |
 42 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 43 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 44 |        // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 45 |        vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 46 |        specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 47 |        //specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 48 |    }
 49 |    
 50 |    // Distancia (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 51 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[0].positionEye), pos);
 52 |
 53 |    // Factor atenuaci칩n
 54 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[0].attenuation[0] + lights[0].attenuation[1] * d + lights[0].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 55 |
 56 |    // Efecto foco
 57 |    float efectoFoco;
 58 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 59 |    {
 60 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 61 |    }
 62 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // V칠rtice fuera del cono iluminado
 63 |    { 
 64 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 65 |    }
 66 |    else
 67 |    {
 68 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 72 |                ( lights[0].ambient +
 73 |                lights[0].diffuse * diffuseMult +
 74 |                lights[0].specular * specularMult );
 75 |
 76 |  return color;
 77 |}
 78 |
 79 |void main()
 80 |{
 81 |
 82 |	if (useParallax) {
 83 |		fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 84 |	} else {
 85 |        vec3 l = normalize(Lvert);
 86 |        vec3 v = normalize(Vvert);
 87 |
 88 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 89 |		vec3 n = normalize(((texture(normales, TexCoord).xyz) - vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)) * 2.0);
 90 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 91 |		
 92 |        fragColor = iluminacion(c, -v, n, v, l);
 93 |	}
 94 |}
 95 |

  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |uniform float scaleFactor;
 26 |uniform float biasValue;
 27 |
 28 |in vec2 TexCoord;
 29 |in vec3 Lvert;
 30 |in vec3 Vvert;
 31 |out vec4 fragColor;
 32 |
 33 |vec4 iluminacion(vec4 color, vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V, vec3 L) {
 34 |
 35 |    // color = Componente emisiva del material
 36 |
 37 |    // L = Vector iluminaci칩n (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 38 |
 39 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 40 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 41 |
 42 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 43 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 44 |        // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 45 |        vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 46 |        specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 47 |        specularMult = pow(specularMult, color);
 48 |    }
 49 |    
 50 |    // Distancia (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 51 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[0].positionEye), pos);
 52 |
 53 |    // Factor atenuaci칩n
 54 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[0].attenuation[0] + lights[0].attenuation[1] * d + lights[0].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 55 |
 56 |    // Efecto foco
 57 |    float efectoFoco;
 58 |    if (lights[0].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 59 |    {
 60 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 61 |    }
 62 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[0].spotCosCutoff) // V칠rtice fuera del cono iluminado
 63 |    { 
 64 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 65 |    }
 66 |    else
 67 |    {
 68 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[0].spotExponent);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 72 |                ( lights[0].ambient +
 73 |                lights[0].diffuse * diffuseMult +
 74 |                lights[0].specular * specularMult );
 75 |
 76 |  return color;
 77 |}
 78 |
 79 |void main()
 80 |{
 81 |
 82 |	if (useParallax) {
 83 |		fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 84 |	} else {
 85 |        vec3 l = normalize(Lvert);
 86 |        vec3 v = normalize(Vvert);
 87 |
 88 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 89 |		vec3 n = normalize(((texture(normales, TexCoord).xyz) - vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)) * 2.0);
 90 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 91 |		
 92 |        fragColor = iluminacion(c, -v, n, v, l);
 93 |	}
 94 |}
 95 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |uniform float scaleFactor;
 26 |uniform float biasValue;
 27 |
 28 |in vec2 TexCoord;
 29 |in vec3 Lvert;
 30 |in vec3 Vvert;
 31 |out vec4 fragColor;
 32 |
 33 |vec4 iluminacion(vec4 color, vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V, vec3 L, float shininess) {
 34 |
 35 |    // color = Componente emisiva del material
 36 |
 37 |    // L = Vector iluminaci칩n (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 38 |
 39 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 40 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 41 |
 42 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 43 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 44 |        // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 45 |        vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 46 |        specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 47 |        specularMult = pow(specularMult, color);
 48 |    }
 49 |    
 50 |    // Distancia (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 51 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[0].positionEye), pos);
 52 |
 53 |    // Factor atenuaci칩n
 54 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[0].attenuation[0] + lights[0].attenuation[1] * d + lights[0].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 55 |
 56 |    // Efecto foco
 57 |    float efectoFoco;
 58 |    if (lights[0].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 59 |    {
 60 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 61 |    }
 62 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[0].spotCosCutoff) // V칠rtice fuera del cono iluminado
 63 |    { 
 64 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 65 |    }
 66 |    else
 67 |    {
 68 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[0].spotExponent);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 72 |                ( lights[0].ambient +
 73 |                lights[0].diffuse * diffuseMult +
 74 |                lights[0].specular * specularMult );
 75 |
 76 |  return color;
 77 |}
 78 |
 79 |void main()
 80 |{
 81 |
 82 |	if (useParallax) {
 83 |		fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 84 |	} else {
 85 |        vec3 l = normalize(Lvert);
 86 |        vec3 v = normalize(Vvert);
 87 |
 88 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 89 |		vec3 n = normalize(((texture(normales, TexCoord).xyz) - vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)) * 2.0);
 90 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 91 |		
 92 |        fragColor = iluminacion(c, -v, n, v, l, b.x);
 93 |	}
 94 |}
 95 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |uniform float scaleFactor;
 26 |uniform float biasValue;
 27 |
 28 |in vec2 TexCoord;
 29 |in vec3 Lvert;
 30 |in vec3 Vvert;
 31 |out vec4 fragColor;
 32 |
 33 |vec4 iluminacion(vec4 color, vec3 N, vec3 V, vec3 L, float b) {
 34 |
 35 |    // color = Componente emisiva del material
 36 |
 37 |    // L = Vector iluminaci칩n (desde v칠rtice a la fuente)
 38 |
 39 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 40 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 41 |
 42 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 43 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 44 |        // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 45 |        vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 46 |        specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 47 |        //specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 48 |    }
 49 |
 50 |    // Efecto foco
 51 |    float efectoFoco;
 52 |    if (lights[0].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 53 |    {
 54 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 55 |    }
 56 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[0].spotCosCutoff) // V칠rtice fuera del cono iluminado
 57 |    { 
 58 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 59 |    }
 60 |    else
 61 |    {
 62 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[0].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[0].spotExponent);
 63 |    }
 64 |
 65 |    color += efectoFoco *
 66 |                ( lights[0].ambient*0 +
 67 |                lights[0].diffuse * diffuseMult * 0.15 +
 68 |                lights[0].specular * specularMult * b * 0.2 );
 69 |
 70 |  return color;
 71 |}
 72 |
 73 |void main()
 74 |{
 75 |
 76 |    vec3 l = normalize(Lvert);
 77 |    vec3 v = normalize(Vvert);
 78 |
 79 |	if (useParallax) {
 80 |        float ht = texture(alturas, TexCoord).x;
 81 |        float h = ht * scaleFactor - biasValue;
 82 |
 83 |        vec2 T_ajustada = TexCoord + h * v.xy;
 84 |
 85 |        vec4 c = texture(colores, T_ajustada);
 86 |        vec3 n = normalize((texture(normales, T_ajustada).xyz - vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)) * 2.0);
 87 |	    vec4 b = texture(brillos, T_ajustada);
 88 |
 89 |        fragColor = iluminacion(c, n, v, l, b.x);
 90 |
 91 |	} else {
 92 |        vec4 c = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 93 |        vec3 n = normalize((texture(normales, TexCoord).xyz - vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)) * 2.0);
 94 |	    vec4 b = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 95 |
 96 |        fragColor = iluminacion(c, -v, n, v, l, b.x);
 97 |	}
 98 |}
 99 |
